',  ', #', Goenka4myChild',  ', #', SmartClasses',  ', #', Innovation', G D Goenka Public School, Lucknow',  added 29 new photos to the album ', Symphony Annual Fete 2016', .',   ', 19 November 2016',   ', \u201cSymphony\u201d, the Three Day Inter-School, spectacular display of cultural activities began on 17th November, 2016. It is a platform where hidden talents come to surface. There was confidence, glee, enthusiasm and a feeling of competition in the air. It was a perfect blend of literary and cultural activities.',  Over seventeen schools from all over the city, participated in various competitions and exhibited their deep-rotted strengths and abilities.',  The Chairman, Mr. Sarvesh Goel ', ...', and the Principal, Ms. Raveen Pande motivated the participants with her encouraging words of appreciation and advice.',  There was a wide range of activities spread out all over the campus at various venues. Some of them are stated as follows \u2013 \u2018Folk Dance\u2019, \u2018Fancy Dress\u2019, \u2018English Recitation\u2019, \u2018Show and Tell\u2019, \u2018Nukkad Natak\u2019, \u2018Spell Bee\u2019, \u2018Newspaper Designing\u2019. The Goan Folk Dance was the talk of the town on the first day. \u2018Fancy Dress\u2019 attracted the audience as the Kindergarten and grade 1 students showcased popular characters from fairy tales like \u2018Pinnochio\u2019 and \u2018The Evil Queen\u2019. On the second day of the event, there was Ramp Walk, Stand-up Comedy, Panorama, Cook Without Fire, Duet Singing and a lot more. ',  Participants were brinaming with confidence and team spirit. They were prompt and overflowing with innovative ideas and techniques.',  G. D. Goenka Public School stood at the first position in \u2018Nukkad Natak\u2019, \u2018Duet Singing\u2019, \u2018Cook Without Fire\u2019, \u2018Group Singing\u2019, \u2018Solo Singing\u2019, \u2018Foot Loose\u2019, \u2018Hindi Debate\u2019 and \u2018Art Attack (Face Painting).',  Lucknow Public School stood first in Mime, Show and tell and Shloak Gayan, Modern Academy in Folk Dance and advice and Mathemagic, Seth A. R. Jaipuria in Fancy Dress, D.P.S. Indira Nagar in Best Out of Waste.',  G. D. Goenka Public School stood second in Mime, Ikebana, Mathemagic and Web-Designing and third in \u2018Shloak Gayan\u2019, Spell Bee, Folk Dance, Spin-A-Yarn and Ad-Mad.',  G. D. Goenka Public School was unbeatable in the solo competitions, as well.',  The Goenkans bagged the first position in Solo stand-up Comedy, Ramp Walk, Solo Singing (English and Hindi), Different strokes and Panorama.',  The overall trophy was grabbed by the students of G. D. Goenka with immense pride and confidence.',  This was followed by a magnificent fete that had stall of games and activities put up by the students of all the classes. The school field was adorned with banners, captions, streamers and various adventure sports like zorbing ball and Rappelling.',  Each stall had its students and teachers who had put forth their best effort in planning interesting games for everyone.',  The purpose of such an event was successfully met as the participants were filled with self-confidence and a drive to participate and perform even better in future.',  ', See more', +26', G D Goenka Public School, Lucknow',  added an ', event', .',   ', 17 November 2016',   ', NOV', 19', Symphony Annual Fete 2016', Sat ', 10:00 UTC+05:30',   ', Lucknow', 47 people interested  68 people going', G D Goenka Public School, Lucknow',  added 27 new photos from 16 November 2016 to the album ', CULTURAL EXTRAVAGANZA \u2018SYMPHONY 2016\u2019 BEGINS AT G.D.GOENKA', .',   ', 16 November 2016',   ',   ', \u201cSymphony 2016\u201d the cultural extravaganza that celebrates childhood year after year began on a note of excitement and expectations at G.D. Goenka School today. A platform where dreams are realised, new records are made, and expressions find fulfillment. A three day inter-school cultural event  extending from 17th November to 19th November, 2016 in which a plethora of activites were organised enabling young aspiring artists to exhibit their inherent talent in a perfect blend o', ...', f literary and cultural activities.',  More than fifteen different schools from the city participated in the various competions, giving the event a colourful, vibrant and enthusiastic start. The Principal, Mrs Raveen Pande addressed the participants, motivating them to showcase their talents on the platform provided. The events scheduled for the morning half of 17th November were \u2018Folk Dance\u2019 ,\u2019Mime\u2019, \u2018Ikebana\u2019, \u2018Fancy Dress\u2019, \u2018English Recitation\u2019, \u2018Zoom in Zoom Out\u2019 and \u2018Show and Tell\u2019. While the events for the latter half of the day included \u2018Best out of Waste\u2019, \u2018Nukkad Natak\u2019, \u2018Spell Bee Junior\u2019 and \u2018Newspaper Designing\u2019.',  The first event for the day was the\u201d Folk Dance Competition\u201d, in which the teams attired in attractive costumes exhibited amazing co-ordination and choreography. Thelavani dance and the Goan folk dances were the highlights of the day. In the \u2018Ikebana \u2013 Flower Arrangement Competition\u2018, the participants had presented colourful creative arrangements with fresh and dry flowers on the themes of \u2018Autumn\u2019, \u2018A joyful birthday party\u2019, \u2019Japanese style of life\u2019, etc. For \u2018Best out of Waste\u2018 the participating teams had shown their ingenuity by producing things like a bangle stand, a lamp, popcorn maker, gift box, an owl in a nest, a flower vase and a photo frame. For\u201d Show and Tell\u201d the children had very innovative ideas along with a very good message for the object they described with a lot of expression. The \u201cSpell Bee Competition\u201d initially began with nine teams which were reduced to six teams for the finals. Though the participants were grilled through the four rounds yet they came out with flying colours. The theme for the \u2018Mime\u2019 was self-defence which the different teams presented in their individual styles. \u2018Nukkad Natak\u2019 or the street play had the theme of Patriotism, the participating teams were in their element and patriotic fervour was at its best here. The \u201cFancy Dress Competition\u2019 for the kindergarten students and grade one had the participants attired as characters from fairy tales like \u2018Pinnochio\u2019, \u2018the Evil Queen\u2019, etc taking one and all to fairyland.',  To give the budding designers of Lucknow a platform, G.D. Goenka Public School organized "Designing with a difference". This competition was a part of the yearly mega event Symphony, a concoction of talent. The students prepared amazing outfits from Newspapers and waste materials. The outfits were inspired by the dream holiday destination Hawaii, capturing the spirit of a Hawaiian girl.The team from GD Goenka chose a theme of a Glass with a heart. They used old CDs and Straws to create their masterpiece. Another team from LPS, South City was described by the words \u201cBelle of the ball\u201d, a dress perfect for the Homecoming night.The competition was judged by Lucknow\u2019s popular socialite Ms Jyotika Mirpuri Aroura.',  With this the events for the day concluded though the students didn\u2019t seem to have had their fill.',  ', See more', +24', G D Goenka Public School, Lucknow',   ', 15 November 2016',   ', Building A Vision For The Future',  ', #', Goenka4myChild', G D Goenka Public School, Lucknow',  with ', Sarvesh Goel', .',   ', 13 November 2016',   ',   ', "G.D. Goenka Public School, Lucknow is a new age school with unique teaching practices, where innovation is the key word, experimentation and new experiences are the norm of everyday work culture and providing education with the latest and choicest techniques introduced in the system is the underlying principle of the school. Using the most modern techniques is our forte and one feels proud of integrating technological advancement in everyday working of the school"- says Mr. ', Sarvesh Goel',   (Chairman), in an interview A three day inter-school cultural event  extending from 17th November to 19th November, 2016 in which a plethora of activites were organised enabling young aspiring artists to exhibit their inherent talent in a perfect blend o', ...', f literary and cultural activities.',  More than fifteen different schools from the city participated in the various competions, giving the event a colourful, vibrant and enthusiastic start.
